# Ticket board вАФ step 2 (proving Theorem 1.2 from the axioms)

Source of truth for the proof phase.  Rationale, DAG, conventions, and wave schedule:
[`step2-plan.md`](step2-plan.md).  The **step-1 board** (statement formalization, ticket IDs
`T-xx` cited in module docstrings) is archived at [`tickets-step1.md`](tickets-step1.md).
Difficulty: в≠Р easy ¬Ј в≠Рв≠Р medium ¬Ј в≠Рв≠Рв≠Р hard/design-sensitive.  Model: **F** = Fable
(design-heavy), **O** = Opus (well-specified).  Status: вШР open ¬Ј вЧР in progress ¬Ј вШС done.

Rules: **no new `axiom`s without explicit user approval** (census at 13 вАФ B10 added by explicit decision, P-06 escalation; B9 base-generalized + B11 added by explicit decision, P-15 escalation, user-approved 2026-07-03; **B11 split into B11a `hilbertSymbol_normCriterion_finiteDyadic` + B11b `unramifiedQuadratic_units_are_norms` by P-23, census 12вЖТ13, user-approved 2026-07-04** вАФ `dyadicNormCriterion` kept as a same-name theorem, spectral-norm bridge isolated as a `def IsUnramifiedQuadraticSpectral`, not an axiom); statement tickets add their sorried theorems to
`SORRY_ALLOWLIST` in `scripts/check_axioms.sh` (same commit, entry cites the ticket), proof
tickets remove them; every ticket's new theorems satisfy `#print axioms` вКЖ std-3 вИ™ the ticket's
**Ax** column; `GQ2/Foundations/Axioms.lean` is frozen; sessions claim a ticket by marking its
row вЧР before starting.  Paper: `paper/A_Profinite_Presentation_for_G__Q_2.pdf`.

## Per-ticket acceptance criteria

Common to all: `lake build GQ2` green; `scripts/check_axioms.sh` green (allowlist edits per the
rules above); `#print axioms` of every new theorem вКЖ std-3 вИ™ the **Ax** column; docstrings carry
paper eq./¬І cross-references; new files, own board row only.

- **P-01** вШС: `docs/STATUS.md` regenerated to the current tree (it stops at 2026-07-02); a script or
  Lean file (`scripts/axiom_ledger.*` or `GQ2/AxiomLedger.lean`) that reports, for every theorem in
  `GQ2`, its non-std-3 axioms, diffable against the per-ticket **Ax** declarations.  Re-run
  instructions in the file header.
  *Done.* `GQ2/AxiomLedger.lean` вАФ a `run_cmd` metaprogram over the elaborated environment
  (`Lean.collectAxioms` per decl; robust to `namespace`/`private`, which the shell
  `.claude/tools/lean4/check_axioms.sh` cannot see).  Re-run: `lake env lean GQ2/AxiomLedger.lean`
  (header documents it; **not** imported by `GQ2.lean`, so `lake build GQ2` never runs it).  Output:
  per-B-axiom consumer lists (diff vs App. D ¬ІC), the `sorryAx` gap map, and an **ALARM** count for
  any other non-standard axiom.  Current run: 613 tracked decls, 601 at std-3, ALARM 0; only B7 has
  consumers (its 6 Euler stress tests), gap map = 6 (the 3 root sorries + 3 transitive).
  `docs/STATUS.md` rewritten as a per-layer ledger (axiom layer, 3-sorry gap map, def-layers
  T-05вА¶T-18, proved infra), with verify-from-scratch commands.
- **P-02** вШС: sorry replaced; **zero sorries in `Reconstruction.lean`**, allowlist entry removed,
  `exists_contSurj_of_card_le`/`reconstruction_of_equinum`/`reconstruction` all `#print axioms` =
  std-3 (`lean_verify`'d), `check_axioms.sh` green (census 10).  Level sets nonempty+finite via
  `contSurj_quotient_nonempty_finite`; the compatible family via `konigFunctor : OpenNormalSubgroup
  (ProfiniteGrp.of R) в•§ Type` + `nonempty_sections_of_finite_cofiltered_system` (K√ґnig), as the
  recipe said.  **Deviation from the recipe's assembly step**: instead of building a cone over
  `ProfiniteGrp.diagram R` and `isLimitCone.lift`, the section is assembled by an **elementary**
  embedding `e : R вЖ™ вИП_U R/U` (closed embedding, `R` compact/`Q` Hausdorff) + **two Cantor
  intersections** (`IsCompact.nonempty_iInter_of_directed_nonempty_isCompact_isClosed`): one in `R`
  realizes each compatible family as `e r` (вЗТ `ѕИ := eвБї¬євИШќ¶` a continuous hom), one in `S` gives `ѕИ`
  surjective.  **Why**: the `ProfiniteGrp.diagram` objects carry the discrete `вК•` topology, not
  `R/U`'s coinduced (equal but not defeq) topology, and `(diagram R).obj U` won't even synthesize a
  `TopologicalSpace` when used as a bare `ContinuousMonoidHom` codomain вАФ so the categorical
  cone/lift route fights Mathlib's `CompHausLike`/`FiniteGrp` coercions at every step.  The
  product-embedding route stays in natural quotient topologies throughout.  Reusable spinoffs (top
  of the file, `open CategoryTheory`): `projMap`(+`_mk`/`_surjective`/`_id`/`_comp_apply`) and
  `konigFunctor` вАФ for **P-04/P-05** (also over `OpenNormalSubgroup (ProfiniteGrp.of _)`).
- **P-03**: `FreeProfiniteGroup X` is t.f.g. for finite `X` (the generators' images topologically
  generate вАФ density of the free group in its completion); t.f.g. passes to `profiniteQuotient`;
  instantiate: `GammaA` t.f.g. in the exact `вИГ s : Finset _, вА¶` form `main_presentation` consumes.
  *Done (`GQ2/FinitelyGenerated.lean`, std-3):* predicate `IsTopologicallyFinGen G` (unfolds to the
  raw `main_presentation` form); `IsTopologicallyFinGen.of_surjective` (transfer along a continuous
  surjection вАФ `DenseRange.topologicalClosure_map_subgroup`); `isTopologicallyFinGen_freeProfiniteGroup`
  (finite `X` вАФ `ProfiniteGrp.ProfiniteCompletion.denseRange` + `FreeGroup.closure_range_of`);
  `gammaA_isTopologicallyFinGen` + `gammaA_topologicallyFinitelyGenerated` (the raw `вИГ`-form P-19 feeds
  to `main_presentation`).
- **P-04** вШС: (i) `tameRelator`/`wildRelator` of `univMarking` lie in `NA` (each dies in every
  admissible quotient вАФ `map_*Relator_eq_one_iff` + `IsAdmissibleU`); (ii) the closed normal
  closure of `{xвВА, xвВБ}`-images in `ќУ_A` is pro-2 (`IsProP 2`, via `MaxProP.lean`'s
  characterization: every open normal subgroup of `ќУ_A` pulls back to an admissible-dominated one вАФ
  the Lemma 2.1 subdirect-closure argument).  Design note documenting the limit argument.
  *Done (`GQ2/AdmissibleLimit.lean`; every theorem `#print axioms` = std-3; no allowlist changes вАФ
  pure proof ticket).*  Deliverables: (i) `tameRelator_mem_NA`/`wildRelator_mem_NA` +
  `quotientMk_*Relator_eq_one` (relations (5)/(6) hold in `ќУ_A`); (ii) `wildCore` (the closed
  normal closure `вЯ®вЯ®xвВА,xвВБвЯ©вЯ©`, on the raw quotient `FвВД вІЄ NA` вЙ°бµИбµЙбґ† `GammaA`) with
  `isProP_wildCore : IsProP 2 wildCore`.  **P-05 interface**: `isAdmissibleU_iff_NA_le`
  (admissible opens = opens above `N_A`) and `generates_univMarking_map` (generation is automatic
  in every finite quotient вАФ density of `FreeGroup` in its completion).  Engine (design note in
  the module docstring): `isAdmissibleU_top` (trivial quotient admissible вАФ nonvacuity without
  App. B) + `isAdmissibleU_inf` (Lemma 2.1 subdirect closure, elementwise 2-power form
  `isPGroup_normalClosure_image_inf`) вЗТ directedness вЗТ compactness domination
  (`exists_isAdmissibleU_le`, the `proPKernel`-style argument) вЗТ `isAdmissibleU_of_NA_le`
  (Lemma 2.2 pushforward).  Lean gotcha recorded: state `wildCore` on `FвВД вІЄ NA`, not
  `Subgroup GammaA` вАФ mixing the `вЖ•GammaA` and raw-quotient spellings breaks instance search
  (`Membership`-instance mismatch), while everything is defeq on the raw type.
- **P-05** вШС: the bijection `ContSurj GammaA G вЙГ {t : Marking G // t.Admissible}` for finite discrete
  `G`: forward = push `univMarking` (admissible by P-04 + Lemma 2.2 `map_admissible`); backward =
  `quotientLift` along `NA_le_ker` (T-21); round-trips via `univMarking_map_toHom` and topological
  generation (P-03).  `Nat.card` conclusion in exactly `main_presentation`'s `hќУA` form.
  *Done (`GQ2/Prop23.lean`; zero sorries; `prop_2_3` and all helpers `#print axioms` = std-3).*
  Headline: `prop_2_3 : Nat.card (ContSurj GammaA G) = admissibleCount G` via
  `contSurjEquivAdmissible` (assembled from named halves `Marking.push`/`Marking.descend` with
  `push_admissible`, `descend_surjective`, `push_descend`, `descend_push`).  Key new lemma:
  `admissible_of_NA_le_ker` вАФ the **converse of `NA_le_ker`** (surjective + `N_A вЙ§ ker` вЗТ pushed
  marking admissible, via P-04's `isAdmissibleU_of_NA_le` + Lemma 2.2 transfer along
  `quotientKerEquivOfSurjective`); together they characterize admissible markings of `G` as the
  continuous surjections `FвВД вЖ† G` killing `N_A`.  **Deviations from this sketch**: (i) t.f.g.
  (P-03) is *not needed* вАФ the round-trip uses the **uniqueness half of the universal property**
  (`Marking.toHom_univMarking_map`: every `f : FвВД вЯґ P` is `toHom` of its own pushed marking;
  CMH-level form `toHom_hom_univMarking_map` via `ConcreteCategory.ofHom`, whose constructor is
  the public route вАФ `ProfiniteGrp.Hom.mk` is private); (ii) the equiv is stated on `FвВД вІЄ NA`
  (defeq `GammaA`, the P-04 spelling convention), `prop_2_3` itself on `GammaA`.  Lean gotchas:
  prove uniqueness by `rw [Marking.toHom, Equiv.symm_apply_eq]` then rewrite
  `homEquiv_apply` **before** `fin_cases i <;> rfl` (otherwise `rfl` unfolds the completion
  adjunction вАФ deterministic timeout), and keep the equiv's fields as *named* lemmas вАФ inline
  `by`-blocks inside the `Equiv` literal retrigger the same timeout via nested-proof abstraction.

  `ќ¶(K)` object: finite ingredients `coatom_normal_of_pGroup` (via `IsPGroup.isNilpotent` +

  all Mathlib) and `coatom_index_of_pGroup` (the coatom quotient is simple by the subgroup

  `IsSimpleGroup.prime_card`); profinite side: `eq_top_of_forall_map_eq_top` (closed subgroup
